de ydropisie	Regarding dropsy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	The cautery does not work in dry conditions, except for the method that is called "asclytes".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis; et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	When you treat according to the methods we have mentioned in sections, and your treatment does not benefit, then it is necessary for you to make four cauteries around the anus, one on the stomach, one on the liver, one on the kidneys, and one behind the back on the spine, and one place on the buttocks; and let the cauteries be well near the spinal nerves where the anus is.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere; et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les .ij. ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	After allowing the cauterization to set for a long time to heal from infection, do not stop the treatment of the disease after the cauterization; and recovery would hasten, with both intentions combined together with God's help.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit; et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	The shape of the cautery for the belly is the blade that we have demonstrated in front; and the one for the back is olive-shaped, as was shown before.
de l’enfleure des piez	regarding the swelling of bones
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire; et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	When the joints are swollen in someone who is anuric and full of yellow bile, it is necessary to apply the cautery on the back between the index finger and the ring finger; and move your hand with the cautery without turning.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too deep through this part, so it would be like leaving the liver, and thus follow this form for the cauterization:
Aprés fai sus .ij. jambes .ij. cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire; et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe; et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse; aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After doing this on both legs, do two cauterizations on each leg at the tip of the heel; and make the cauterizations long, one in front of the knee joint and the other behind, halfway along the leg; and leave the cauterizations alone for a long time without treating them until the yellow bile comes out; after that treat all the other treatments we have mentioned.
de la menoison	Of the memory
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures; et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai .i. grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule; et .iiij. cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout .i. cautere clavile subtil, et .ij. cauteres sus les hainches.	For ailments of the stomach that come from cold and moisture, as long as the retaining and digestive virtues which are in the stomach and intestines are weakened, they cannot be cured by ordinary treatment methods; and you see the patient suffering greatly with strong green symptoms, so apply one large stomach cautery according to what has been discussed earlier or stomach cautery, with a circulating cautery; and four internal abdominal treatments around the mouth of subtle substances for each. Then apply one delicate hip cautery and four cauterizations on the thighs.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et .i. cautere sus chaicun yle, et .ij. petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see abundant moisture and the patient suffering, apply a cautery to the wrist, and one cautery on each knee, and two small cauterizations on the stomach below the large ones, because the treatment benefits when there is good help.
de la cure des emorroydes	Of treatments for hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres: III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois; et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile; et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	When the hemorrhages are at their origin or multiple and are old with large cold, moist, corrupted fluids, and they are treated as we have said in divisions, but if it does not benefit, then do cauterizations: III on the spine of the back, that is right beyond the middle point somewhat into the muscle little by little in a triangular pattern, and one cauterization under the liver II inches; and if you think the stomach has cooled down and the meat doesn't cook, and you see it swell, then apply I large cauterization on the stomach as previously mentioned, and another on the liver, and another on the spleen with all the cauterizations. And let the cauterization last for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treatment until it is healed.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	Regarding the disease called "thelul".
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble .i. raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit; et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort; fai ceu une fois ou .ij., et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit; aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez; et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	When you are working with the shoulder, heat the tool that seems to be a rasp until it is glowing hot, and then place all of its heated part on the shoulder being worked; let your hand remain as long as the cautery touches the beginning of the vein from which blood flows. Perform this action once or twice, and if there are many shoulders, cauterize each one as we have said; after applying ointments for benefit, do so while they are still in good condition; and if you use a large cautery on the shoulder blade, it will provide more help.
de plaie mal curee	of improperly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot endure surgery or opening (operation), which we will describe in its proper place, should such a disease occur that cannot be cured except by cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	If there is no瘘管, it becomes old and festers with corrupted moisture, so you should thoroughly inspect the area for any sign of a subtle change. And remember that you need to know precisely how far up the test needs to go.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	After the scrape, apply a cauterizing agent that seems appropriate, and insert it into the fistula according to the depth of its entry point. Reapply the cauterizing agent until the diseased pus is no longer burned away, once or twice, depending on your need; and be cautious not to burn nerves or large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	If the fistula extends to the bladder or the intestine, be aware of these symptoms and do not perform this procedure outside their natural location. Remember that the cure should only be done inside their natural place, and consider that it is not a normal condition. After treating until the area heals, if the wound has healed over completely, know that the treatment was successful; and if the tissues are not hardened after an extended period of time, realize that the wound is still open and the bones have become rotten at its base, like in one of these examples we will discuss in their natural place.
de la maladie des reins	Of kidney disease
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit; et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra .iij. cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	When abdominal pain originates from the kidneys and large wind, it affects women differently, hence you should apply a cautery to both sides of the kidneys with a bistoury as we have previously mentioned; if we cauterize in the middle, there will be three cauterizations in line, and they will provide more help.
de la vessie	From the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et .i. a destre et .i. a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce; et li fais .i. cautere defuers le dos, ou .ij. se tu en as besoing; et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	When the bladder is thick and weak from heat and moisture such that patients retain urine, then the physician should perform a cautery on the lower part of the bladder, where the body hair begins, and one each on the right and left sides, and make sure each cauterization spans as long as it takes about an inch; and if necessary, also do a cauterization behind the back, or two if needed; and perform the cauterizations in a cross pattern according to the form described beforehand.
de la marris	From the mare's milk
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde; et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor: adonques covient il c’on li faice .iij. cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et .ij. cauteres defuers le dos; et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	When the mare's milk is cold and moist, and does not allow for conception, and its flowers are corrupted causing delayed periods; and when they do come, one can feel great pain: in such a case, it would be appropriate to perform three cauterizations inside the uterus, as we have described or like how we explained for bladder cautery, and two cauterizations behind the back; and make sure the cauterizations are done in a cross pattern, as we have said.
de la hainche	From the thigh
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble; et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a .i. cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle; et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	When the viscous fluids descend into the thigh cavity, and because of this reason it moves out of its place, and the signs are that the leg is longer than the other when measured together; and you find the joints at their starting points visible. It should be that you cauterize the disease on the thigh around .i. the appearance of a circle, and mark in front of the joint along the thigh as it curves, so that the thigh is within the circle; and if they are like those which have been cauterized for stomach issues.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai .iij. cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if these cauterizations do not seem present, make three large olive-like cauterizations, and let the cauterizations be as long as all the ribs; and treat until it is healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	From thigh pain
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene: adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	When pain comes in the buttock region, and this is due to coldness and moisture, and the patient is treated according to what we have discussed about divisions and treatment, but the cure does not work, and the disease is old: then it must be that you cleanse the patient of the thick fluids using stinking pills, or other similar good pills.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	After you perform the cautery; and the method of how to do the cautery is according to two methods: this means together with burning substances, and fire cautery.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz: que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire; aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Fire cautery has several methods, among which one is like this: you should cauterize the buttock area with three triangular cauterizations following this shape, and make each cauterization deep and large, leaving an interval between each cauterization equivalent to the size of two coins, and use olive oil as the cauterization substance; no cauterization should be done in the middle of the buttocks because according to this form there are four cauterizations.
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you see fit, apply the circle cautery method that we described earlier regarding the dislocation of the buttock; but make sure the circles encompass the entire buttock area and all parts of the wound are heated through.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	This is the way it's done in sciatica, when pain stays in the buttocks and doesn't reach up to the thigh or leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc; et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur; et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And if it comes up to the thigh and leg, make two fire cauteries there where the patient says the pain holds them back, and four above the ankle on each side a bit more to the left; and have the surgical cuts, and burn off the thickenings of the heel; and if the patient feels that the pain extends down to four or even five feet or just before the knee, cauterize where they feel the pain three points or four with the ‘point’ type of cautery.
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if there's more work needed, then you proceed with more cauterizations; and if it is that the pain spans from the knee towards the thigh, then do a circular or knife-like cauterization, and be sure to well maintain your caution throughout all your cauterizations so as not to leave any part undone, burning nerves and large arteries until they are properly treated, and do not cause the patient more harm or contraction than necessary.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen many who performed a cautery on the ankle up to the knee, and they only allowed it until the leg was completely swollen, and also all the feet, causing them to be pierced and corrupted throughout.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After an abdominal treatment that led to their death.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pains are in two parts together, make a cautery on each one, according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c’est li forme:	And the sage said about the cautery of the hip, as follows: make it such that the iron is at the top as big as a chicken's head, or perhaps slightly smaller, and place it between supports and have it in between each support stretching from one end to the other, the size of a pea; let the supports be divided into two parts, and they should resemble knots too, and ensure the iron handle is well made; this is its form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit; et lou cauterize une fois .i. cautere reont et lou laisse .iij. jors; et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens; aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	And heat it until it is completely red and emits steam, then place it on the area of concern at the hip gland, and rotate around the healthy ribs; and apply one cautery treatment with repeated applications every day for three days; and then cover the affected area with butter, allowing the wound to be exposed as long as needed; after the ointment treatment until it has healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent; et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	Albucasim says that we use very little of this cautery for his fear of the effects, and we find few who use it; yet this is a good type of cautery, which can be tolerated, and there where it takes effect.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	The burning medical cauteries are such that you make an instrument with supports in which the edge of the door descends, and it can be made of steel or iron with a long side, and at the height have two knots, and between each one have the size of a pea; let them be over a fire and above too, and join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche; aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After applying the balm to the buttocks of the lying patient on a firm surface, hasten your hand to the area of the buttock. Next place between the two circles of the hot embers which are heated in fire, and allow one hour exactly, then permit the patient to endure the heat and burning sensation.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu; et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit; et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait; et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	For there one finds biting like that of fire; and when the bite passes, lift your hand with the tool and elevate the buttock gently from the embers. And leave it for three days, and put on butter until what is blackened by scorching turns to ash; and let it be for three days as long as pus has come out. And this would be the last aid after the removal of ointments while he remains sound.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument; et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	And if the pain has spread up to the thigh or even to the leg, you should apply a heated instrument there in accordance with what you have done on the hip also; and this is how you use hot leeches, and I have written about correcting medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take ashes and quicklime in equal amounts of one to the other, grind them together, and put them into a new jar.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir; et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main; et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	Let it have the shape of a small reed so that the point of a razor may be able to enter; and put this jar into another one well filled with water, and place ashes and lime in gently until there are two inches above the powders when you will have taken them gently by hand; and leave it like this until all the water turns into liquid and sediment or is completely covered, then take all of this liquid, and pour it over lime and over ashes as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	And thus it will be very effective and administered in the movements of medical works and other members' cauteries. For she accomplishes a work like fire, and to others medicines whereby one cauterizes well the hip bone so as with tannisia and melon seed oil, walnut and soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galen tells us of a treatment in which an honored person was treated for the pain in the hip and sciatic vein, and with great relief. He says that no other treatment was done, and that it cured him completely in one fell swoop when this treatment was performed, and he bathed himself as he instructs hereafter.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie; et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	And it is said in this manner that you take some green and dry argyrite dust, grind it thoroughly with a little fat, and place it on the hip, thigh and leg where the pain occurs, then tie it up; and let him leave it for three hours until the patient no longer feels the burn.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then make them enter into a bath as long as their body becomes somewhat refreshed, and make them enter onto bed, and the pain will disappear completely and they shall be healed.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	Know that no one should use such medicines as a cautery, if it isn't after the removal of flesh.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout; et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	And Dioscorides states that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with donkey's fat, if it helps much; and the cautery should be made in this manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take lard and mix it with old oil, and place it on the hollow area between the base of the thumb and the other that is called a flexor.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains; et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee; et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	After taking donkey hair and let it burn until it turns to charcoal, put it on the lard, and leave it until it sticks; and repeat this process again, never stopping until you think it will reach up to the hip bone, and that pain is gone; and this method of cautery is called "donkey's hair cautery".
de la dolor dou dos	The pain of the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether by falling or impact, or due to too much evacuation, or because of cold matter spread out, none of these occurrences warrants cauterization, rather it is for someone who has come from an infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne .v. cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir; et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»; et se tu vues, fai .iij. cauteres ou .iiij. au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	It is necessary after this that when the body has been cleared of putrid pills or other such occurrences, one should place on the back where the pain resides, three lines marked with a cross, and in each line, up to .v. cauterizations according to the power and quantity that the body can endure; and perform the cauterization as per the "point" cautery named; and if you see fit, do .iij. or .iiij. cauterizations at the intermediate "claw" cautery in accordance with this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor; et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	This illness often befalls children and at the beginning of its manifestation, it shows itself in that they are pale when they stand up, and fear follows; and you find in the last spinal bone of the back and on us, an appearance that comes over other bones.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and observe it being treated, if you apply the fire cautery according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	If the fire cautery is applied to each part of the spine equally.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see fit, apply the fire cautery to each side of the spine with two or three lines of heat, and ensure the points are close together.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After the treatment until it is clean according to what we have said, and be careful not to apply heat in a state of fever where there might be nerve inflammation.
de la dolor des jointes	of joint pain
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When joint pain is caused by moist substances spreading throughout the body's limbs, and when pain comes in feet which people call 'gout' properly, and when it is due to cold reasons and its cure needs medicines that cannot be treated, then it should be treated with cauteries in this manner: create the cautery at the joint of the foot, and let the olive oil cautery take this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there's need that you touch the back of the foot, if it is heated to the full heat of what we call 'a point'.
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if the pains extend to the knees and other joints, and this happens many times, then apply heat to each knee with three or four parts of each side, over the entire olive heat; and if you need more, do so more, but don't remove your hand until as much of the heat as is good for the knee has been applied.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains go down to the knees and back, then administer the cautery as we have said in our chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pains are in the hands, make points between the inner wrist lines II; and if there remains any pain on the wrists, make points on each joint and on the hair of the hand; and if the pains come up to the elbows or shoulders, cauterize each part, and take good care of the patient and apply remedies.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	And if you take good care of him and cleanse the humor, he will be helped by God to recovery.
de la routure dou syfac	Of the rupture of the spleen
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When an opening comes in the stomach, and the intestines descend into the abdomen it is newly so; it must be that when you see them being cured, they do not eat until noon; and use things which let the wind out, so that their insides descend from their belly; after make him sit on his back between your hands, and command him to shave his armpit until the intestines are repaired, then take them in your fingers, and observe around the opening above the bone, and take it by the root of the intestine. Then apply the cautery as described here:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	Until it is white and emits pus.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Then remove the boils from their place; and let the attendants prick his hand so that they do not turn back; and work well on the thighs for the patient, and apply I crutch and I sergeant to the thighs, and another under his buttocks where you pinch his hands; then put the cautery on every sign on your whole hand, and hold it straight until you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, repeat it again as many times as necessary until you reach the bone; and be careful that the boil does not spill when you apply the cautery; that you do not burn him; and that this way the patient does not suffer or any other harms.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that when you do not reach bone with the cautery, your operations are worthless.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	And it must be that the cauteries for children are delicate according to their size, and also large according to their size; after three days cleanse the limb with a balm until the scab is removed; then apply other ointments until it heals well, and let them rest on their back for forty days so that the wound heals properly; and their convalescence should be extended long enough so that the pus does not overflow when they wish to walk in rooms.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	And after forty days, when they wish to stand up, help them with a well-made bandage and keep it on for another forty days; and give him good rest, have him work little and guard against overconsumption of drinking and eating, and loud shouting; and when he performs this exercise, he will be completely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say after about the treatment of tailoring in this chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	Of the rupture of the abdomen
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	And when incisions occur in other bellies and are known, and you see that they no longer grow, make the cautery with the cautery repeatedly according to its quantity, and apply it for one-third of the measure; after treat them as we have said; and none of the old ones said that one should cauterize at the cautery in three angles according to this form:

Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauterizations are lighter and more moist.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	from old pain in no limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes to any limb, or due to falling or being hit, and this pain lasts for a long time, and medical treatment does not help, then it must be cauterized with the cautery called "points", and apply the cauterizations according to the length of the limb, its smallness, its weakness, its utility, and its location of twists and its pain.

If the first treatment with heat was successful, that's good; if not, try another heat treatment on this one, because such treatments require movement close to the affected body part, so you should perform the heat treatments as long as the wounds are healthy.
de meselerie	In mixture
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The remedies are administered once per heat treatment by great help, and similarly, the disease comes from the putrefaction of blood and melancholy.

Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et .i. cautere en som lou neis, et .ij. cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et .vj. cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et .i. grant sus la crupie et .i. autre delez, et .ij. sus les .ij. espaules; et .ij. sus les coutes, et .ij. sus les tendrons dou pis, et .i. sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et .i. autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et .i. autre sus lou foie. And know that the more I apply the cautery, the more help I provide, and it benefits them; and know that patients do not feel pain from the cautery as healthy individuals do, because their bodies are already completely corrupted.

Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After treatment, wash the wound with flour mixed with honey and other remedies until it heals properly.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	When there is swelling in any limb that is treated with medicines and oils, and it doesn't heal properly, then apply cautery to the limb according to the size of the limb; and let the cautery enter slightly into the skin at the site of the wound; then treat it with ointments until it heals.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure; et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	And always make the cautery and on the hand and foot and back, at the exit of the nerve that paralyzes the limb, and thus is extracted the swelling; and no one should interfere with it unless they are knowledgeable about the limbs and the exits of the moving nerves in the body.

When the illness named "albaras" becomes old, and conventional medicine is ineffective, then apply a small cautery burn according to the amount of the plant in question. li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment for a pustule by cauterization

Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres. li cure dou feu par fer	The cure using fire through a iron
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another way of disease is called 'corrodens', and it's not another thing but a member infirmity, for it causes members to behave as if they were dry branches that the fire has burnt.

des porrelz qui vienent as piez	Of ulcers that come on bones

Sometimes, when there is an opening in the foot, it leads to a disease that we call "closed" according to our understanding, and it is a large hard lump that causes pain in the foot.

C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	This is to know about fire cautery, and hot water cautery.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges; aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou; et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture; puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	The fire cautery involves heating it up, and the metal cautery is shaped like a feather, made of good iron to be able to touch all parts of the nail, with thin margins; after heating it fully on the nail, turn your hand completely around the nail until it reaches the end of the nail; then leave it like this for three days until the process begins to create pus; then make an application of mixed fat poultices with lard and let the poultice stay overnight, and the nail will fall out and be uprooted from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the wound with greasing until it is clean.

And if they have turned under the breast and occur many times in hands and elbows, it's necessary that you bring them the cautery of hot water; and follow this manner: take one from an aragon or iron, or a feather of a goose, and place it on the nail and the thorn, meaning to say for warts; and place the stick so that its entire surface is touched by flame, then add a little hot water, hold your hand well, press your hand back until the edge of the stick burns to the root of the nail, and then find the hot water flowing deeply down to the root; and let the patient endure for an hour the irritation from the hot water; then leave him like that, and it will uproot everything at its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Do this for one after the other, until you have cleared all those that are in your body, then treat the sores that generate pus.
li cure dou trembler	The treatment involves shaking it off.

When someone shakes from cold or nerves, or has a fever that lasts four days or another condition, it is necessary to apply four or four cauterizations on the spine of their back, one cautery between each vertebra; and one on the chest at the olive-shaped cautery; if this does not stop the shaking, then hasten the recovery from the cold illness.
des pustules puans	The pus-filled lesions
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	In every instance where a dead body is exposed or oozing sores, or pus-filled bumps appear, these come from large putrid materials.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	When they become apparent that one must apply a cautery to each head of the pustule: a delicate firewood stick from the myrtle tree, with its tip grasped by the flame, or from the long root of aristolochia, or with the lens-shaped cautery.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez; mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	And in every instance when they are cauterized at the beginning once they become apparent, following this manner, and it cannot grow any pus forwards but the excess which causes them is removed, and they become clean; but it must be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	When the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses; et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	Many times great amounts of blood have flowed from the artery that has been cut at the wound when it comes to the one going beyond, or incision of an abscess, or the cautery on the limb, and similar things; and it is very troublesome a matter to stanch.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus; puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge; puis empren .i., ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	And yet, when this happens to none of them, should you quickly place your index finger on the wound of the vein and press very much until the pain subsides under your finger, and no more drops flow; then apply several small and large olive oil cauteries as long as they are all red. Then take .i., or large or small depending on the wound and to the place where the artery is located, and place the cautery on that vein where you hold your finger, and keep the cautery there until the pain stops completely.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement .i. autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if it jumps out when you remove your finger from the vein, and once the cauteries are extinguished, take quickly another one of the cauterizing tools that are at the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez; et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide; et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des .iiij. manieres que nos avons dit: ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc; et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And do not stop performing this one after another until the skin is completely incised; and beware that you do not burn the nerve underneath it, nor let any other harm come upon the patient; and know that when hair falls from the artery, one cannot properly incise it even if the artery is large, unless done through one of the four methods we have mentioned: by cautery, or extraction when it hasn't been treated yet, or by strong stringing where a ligature is placed, or with medicines applied which have the power to incision blood; and it should be bound and held in place subsequently.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Who will administer the tying or binding with cloths tightly or by putting heat-bearing things thereon, or other similar actions, if it doesn't prove effective.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne; et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez; et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And if this happens to anyone and they have no means or medicine at hand, then they should place their index finger on the wound of the vein as we said, and stretch it well until the skin is incised over the wound and over the vein; and do not move the hand but moisten it with cold water often that remains very cold until the skin is frozen and swollen and incised; and perform ligatures in advance for those requiring cautery and medicines.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	This begins the second book of treatments for amputations
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres; et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	We have spoken in the first chapter about all diseases where it is necessary to use fire cautery or hot medicine. We discussed their uses, causes, instruments and forms of cautery; and concluded that chapter with applying them up to the foot, and I will proceed through this chapter using the same path since it seems easier to find what one wants here.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And when I begin this, it is important for you to understand that in this chapter there is more risk and fear than in the first section about using cautery, and for this reason, greater caution is required.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses; ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and treating wounds, and extracting arrows, and making cuts into stones, and similar matters; where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I advise you not to undertake foolishness.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many ways of people come to treatments.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice; et de ces doit on avoir paor.	Some come from those who are so afflicted by their disease that they die lightly due to the panic they find in their illness, and the severity of their suffering; and for this one must have fear.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit: «atendez, je sui garis»; et li maladie est despitouse.	And among these there is someone who gives its meaning and says: "Wait, I am a liar"; and the illness is deceitful.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los; et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie; et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	It is not fitting that you should agree with those who come to you in this manner, but rather place greater caution in your honor than in your greed, and do not rashly open your mouth but wisely of those whom you are certain, and from whom you have taken knowledge; use prediction and indication in the treatment of your sick for whose salvation it is turned; and this will help you to acquire good reputation, glory, and lasting memory.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Dear child, our lords give you good understanding and justice, and if you wish to aspire from the holy inspiration of their hand, Amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Or I have instructed this chapter according to its chapters, following what is before it in the section on cauteries, which I have outlined from the head down to the feet because you will find them more easily than those you need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	From the head full of water
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant; et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	Know that this illness comes very often to children at birth, and when the mother presses too hard on the head of the child; and it happens in no other case for reasons unknown.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors; et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	And I have never seen this disease in anyone other than children, and among all those I've seen, their deaths came quickly; for this reason, it seems to me that I should abandon the treatment of cases like these with partial cures.
Et je vis .i. enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir; et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os; et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large; et soit ausi longe com .ij. nous, tant que li mostor corre; et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	And I saw one child whose shoulder joints were filled with water, and his head grew each day to the point where he could not bear it anymore; and feared so much from moisture that he died, and this moisture is assembled around the bone above the siphon, between the heart and the bone; and the veins are arranged in such a way when moisture is between the heart and the bone, and abscesses are small, that you make an opening under the head a large crack; and so long as the moisture flows; and see this shape of the spathile:
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai .ij. fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more abundant, and the abscess is larger, make two openings in a manner like a cross, according to this shape:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut: si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief .iij. fendures selonc ceste maniere:	And if the moisture is within the bone, and the signs you see show that the edges of the head have opened from every part, and water spurts out when you press it inward with your hand, and this does not stop: then you should make three openings in the middle of the head like this:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, extract all the moisture completely.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor; puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	After holding the cuts from cloths and powders, and I place wine and oil, and let this way up to the fifth day; then I remove it, and treat the wound with bandages and ointments, and let the head also be held in place equally, and finally allow the patient to eat dry meat of a bit moist until the limb is strengthened and healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue; car aucune fois est elle devant; aucune fois derrier; aucune fois en destre; et aucune fois en senestre.	And another way of incision is that you look at where the opening of the abscess is large, and assemble with water; because it does not always appear in front; nor always behind; nor always on the right side; nor always on the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir; et warde que tu ne coper l’artere; et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	Cut then where the abscess opens, and fill with water, and make a cut according to what you can do; and watch that you do not cut the artery; and look for a flow of blood, so that the patient dies due to the loss of blood and evacuation of moisture.
de reume	Of cautery by fire, command to the unwell that they let the hairs grow long and even; and if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les .ij. arteres.	When there occurs a disease which is called "catarrh" to the eyes or at the bottom (of the body), and the disease is old, and the treatment with medicine doesn't help, then the last resort of treatment could be cautery using what one would cauterize their two major arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief; aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel; puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues; puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	So then, so that you can handle them properly, the patients must stand after their head; after rubbing their face with a rough cloth until the arteries are visible, then remove the patient's neck up to all parts of the cloth; then look where the veins lie, and the positions of the ears from one side to the other, and they are restored; then mark both ears, then apply each with an extremely sharp knife blade for half of them, until the cut reaches the bone, and this should be done in accordance with the width of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com .ij. dois au traver.	And if you see it, stop the bleeding from beneath the artery and above the cut, by making a cut also like one inch through.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, let the blood flow out continuously from up top.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os; et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere; puis regarde la plaie: s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	And if the artery doesn't open upon feeling, it is necessary that you measure the size of the space to three fingers, then press and push until touching the bone; and what needs to be extracted from blood is six c/, and by chance a little more or less depending on how the patient can endure, and the filling of the artery; then look at the wound: if it remains above the bone point like syphac, if the abscess in the incision doesn't appear, then press the wound and tie it, and the ointment cure until it heals.
de emigrainne	Of the removal
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When old age comes, and acute cough, because of the moisture from tears and heat in the temples and lower back that is beyond endurance and similar things. Medicine is treated with ways of medicinal cures and all this does not help him, so we extract the arteries in the temples and cauterize them, as we have reported.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit; et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement; puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	And the method of extracting them is such that one feels beneath their temple hair, and hears about the artery that opens in the temple, for it opens well by its pulsation, and is only responsive in some who are too cold; and if it responds, then strain his neck with some cloth strips, then rub the area with a rough cloth, and heat him up with hot water until the artery becomes clearly evident. Then take the spatula as shown below:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie; et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	Then scrape the skin gently until you feel the artery, then pull it upwards with forceps, and remove all threads that are in each part; and if the artery is thin, if you turn it to the tip of the hook, then trim that part according to the size of two fingers.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it isn't cut, or jumps not all at once,
Et trai dou sanc des .vj. c/, jusc’a .iij.; et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en .ij. leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc; puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les .ij. liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez; et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	And drain the blood from the .vj. c, until the third day; and if the artery is large, then it should be tied in two loops of a strong double thread of silk, so that infection does not occur before the healing of the wound, nor repeatedly bleed; then cut off the excess between the two threads at that moment, and then, if you see, then apply the cautery gently until the bone with the bones being cut; and this is the surgical procedure, should the patient not have fever and be of warm complexion.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors: por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	For the cautery helps to finish off infections: for this reason it is a greater help against infections.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites; et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez; et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez; et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient; et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de .ij. pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	When it comes to extracting arteries, one must fill the area with old cotton and place well-made tent cloths over it; when you sever them, apply dry medicinal substances that promote tissue growth, as well as tent cloths until it heals. And if you don't have a proper clamp for the artery, act just as you would during extraction, hurry to use a cautery tool, or utilize the area with vitriol and grip your hand tightly so that the clot stays in place; and if you lack this present tool, apply ice on the clot until it freezes, then immerse the affected area in cold water until the clot no longer moves, ensuring proper restraint. The one who is faster and lighter during artery extraction should cauterize the blood vessel from that cautery trenching for half an inch, but make sure the trenching is well spaced to retain heat for a longer duration.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the instruments are too tight, they retain less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les .ij. coutelz .i. doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les .ij. leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en .ij. leus; et soient esloigniet entre les .ij. chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout; et c’est li forme dou cautere:	And there should be .i. inch of space between the two knives, and when you have heated them to touch both ends, place the hot iron until it reaches the bone, then cauterize the vessel in two places; and keep them spaced apart for these shoulder joints because there is no soldering on this cautery tool throughout; and this is the shape of the cautery:
des larmes	of tears
Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis; et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	When tears of the eyes are descending through the veins that are above the testicle of the head of the arm, and it does not benefit from any treatment with medicine that one might do, and you see the face of the patient turning red, and feel or see a pulsation as if of a heartbeat; and where they are tender and moist so that the hairs on paper fall off, and the papers become heated, and burned by the heat of the tears, it is necessary to have this treatment.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front; et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres; et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins; et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	And they called the old "bruise cure", and if you treat someone with this illness by having hair on their head or forehead, then make three cuts evenly across the forehead according to the length of the forehead; and make one cut like two lengths all along the forehead from below upwards until it stops near the nose, and the other two cuts like two lengths above the eyebrows, making sure not to cut the arteries that are above the eyebrows; keep your hand away from the continuation of the two jaws, and each wound should be the size of three finger widths in width; have a piece of sponge and some cloth ready to wipe off any blood, then use the sharp instrument that is formed from two parts.
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision; et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les .ij. fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.	from the cut that is near the temple up to the second cut; and burn all the flesh that is between the two gaps evenly until it sticks to the bone, then make another cut from the middle cut up to the other gap, and then extract this ague brazier.
si boute en la premiere fendure l’estrument qui est apelez «cultellaire», et est tresbien trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part est souef, ne mie trenchans, et c’est li forme:	if you ignite in the first gap the tool called 'cultellaire', and it is very sharp on one side, but blunt on the other, it has this shape:
Et met le costeit taillant vers la char aerse au keur, et lou costeit souef vers l’os, et lou boute tant qu’il veigne a la moiene fendure.	And make the cut towards the fatty part of the meat at the bone, and the cut should go towards the bone from the flesh, and stop when it feels halfway through the skin.
Et cope toz les vasselz que dessendent dou chief as eulz tant que l’incision soit continue jusc’a ceu qui apert dou keur, et puis autreteil fai en la moiene fendure jusc’a l’autre defuer; et puis estrai dou sanc igalment, et espresse lou leu por le sanc pris; puis met en chescune fendure une tente de viel coton, et met sus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile et en aisil, et garde que apostemes chaus n’i veigne; et au tier jor deslie lou liien, et i amenistre grant planteit d’aigue tede, puis lou cure d’oignement basilicon avec oile roset, et d’autres cures dont on cure plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And remove all the veins that descend from the head as far as possible until an incision is made through to the flesh; and then proceed similarly in the middle of the cut up to the other opening. And then extract equal blood evenly, press out the flesh for the taken blood; then place a patch of old cotton in each incision, and apply wet cloths soaked with wine and oil and garlic, making sure no pus is seen; and on the third day release the bandage, and provide ample cool water, then administer a cure with ointment basilico mixed with rose oil, and other treatments used for wounds until it heals.
dou reume des eulz	of the eyes
Quant a aucun vienent catarre agut acostumeement, et tu vois les eulz tenves et petis, et afoiblir la veue, et les papieres brulees; et li poil chieent, et ou chief en parfont a dolor ague, et li malaides esternue; adonques saiches par ces accidens que celles matieres et cil catharre ne vient fuer que de maintes voines, et li muedre cure que i est, si est ceste.	When there is an acute catarrh accustomed, and you see the eyes swollen and small, and weakening of sight, and burnt paper; and hair falls out, and one feels a feverish chill, and the patient sneezes. Therefore, know from these events that those substances and this mucus come only from many veins, and the remedy used, if it is such.
Et est que tu comande au malaide a rere son front, puis fai une grant fendure emmi lou front, et une autre dou large I poc.	And it is that you instruct the patient behind their forehead, then make a large cut in the middle of the forehead, and another one somewhat wide below this.
Et comence des la fendure de la temple senestre a la temple destre, et soit li incision jusc’a l’os; et esloigne ta main des ners des temples que muevent au mengier; et quant li os est descovers, si essue tout le sanc a une esponge, et puis desevre entre les II levres de la fendure et i met coton viel, et tentes de lin; puis lie desus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile, et te garde d’aposteme chaut; quant il est ostez, si covient que tu frottes l’os tant que chars i comence a naistre, puis le cure de choses exiccatives, que font enjanrer char. des poilz des papieres	The phrase "des poilz des papieres" translates directly to "the hairs of papers". This might refer to paper fibers or could be metaphorical depending on context. Without more information, this is the literal translation.
Quant em papieres naissent poilz ajostez autre que li naturez, et sont enveillit, si nuisent as eulz, et font venir manieres de maladies si com larmes acostumees et mollifications des papieres et albugine, tant que c’est cause de la destruction des eulz; et est li cure selonc .iiij. manieres: ou par cautere ensamble feu, ou par medicine ague selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre de cautere, et est fais ou par incision et costure ou par caines, selonc ceu que je dirai. de la porriture de l’oil	Regarding eye infections
