And when they are brought back equally, and the mouth of the patient is well closed with mild soothing, then place damp cloths on a paste made from rose oil and beeswax, then bind it lightly with moist string; and have the patient lie on their back, and their limbs between two cushions, so that they do not move neither to the right nor to the left, nor try to twist themselves more, but require light food, until the pains are subdued, and the jaws are stitched up; and then allow them to eat lightly, without opening their mouth while eating or drinking, until the jaw is well stitched up and healed.
Et se les .ij. mandibules ne pueent estre remises a point a une houre, et ne sont mie converties a lor leus, si en vient fievres et sode acostumees, et par aventure solution de ventre, et par aventure vomist cole pure.	And if the two mandibles cannot be properly aligned within an hour and are not converted back to their original positions, then fevers and recurrent swelling occur, along with occasional abdominal discomfort, and occasionally, vomiting of pure fluids.
Et quant tu verras ceu, adonc saiches que c’est perdicions; et maintes fois muert cil cui il avient, en .viiij. jors.	And when you see this, then know that it's a loss; and many times, death occurs to the one who experiences this within seven days.
de la forcelle	from the lever
Li forcele ne puet desaluer dou costeit dedens la continuation de li et dou pis, et est desaluee aucune fois au defuer, et bien le sent on.	The strength cannot relieve from within the middle of the back and at its base, and is dislocated outwards every time, and one feels this well indeed.
Et li restauration si est que li malaides gise sovin sor son dos, et estende ses bras; et puis presse le leu forment a ta palme, et elle revenra; puis met sus l’emplaustre et lou bendeil, et l’estraint; et li chiez qui est devers lou coute ne puet desaluer; se poc non, et se il desalue aucune fois, si le ramoinne a son leu, si com nos avons dit; puis met sus l’emplaustre et le bendeil, et l’estraint, et coumande au malaide qu’il se repose tant qu’il soit sanez; et ensi meisme est ramenez li chiés de l’espale, quant il est desevrez de son leu.	And the restoration is such that the patient lies still on their back, and extends their arms; then press into your palm the shape of their body, and it will return; then put them onto the plaster and bind them, and tighten; and if they dislocate again towards the cut, do not allow them to move; should they, and if they dislocate once, you must reset it back in place as we have said; then put them onto the plaster and bind, and tighten, and instruct the patient to rest until healed; and thus similarly are returned the shoulders of the spine when they are removed from their place.
de la dislocation de l’espaule	Concerning the dislocation of the shoulder
Saiches que li espaule n’est desaluee fuer que selonc III manieres: de coi l’une est qu’ele desalue a la partie de l’assele au desoz; et li seconde est a la partie dou pis; et par aventure desalue a la partie desus, et ceu avient poc; et ne desalue mie derrier por l’espaule, et ne desalue mie dedens por les ners; et plusors fois desalue desoz vers l’assele, meismement a ces qui ont poc de char, car a ces saut ele fuer hastanment; a ces qui ont assez char, saut ele a poines, et rentre a poines.	Know that the shoulder is dislocated according to three ways: one way it dislocates from the part of the acromion down to the base; and the second way it dislocates from the part near the heel; and accidentally it dislocates upwards, which happens rarely; it does not dislocate behind for the shoulder, nor inwards for nerves; and it dislocates downwards towards the acromion multiple times, even for those with little flesh; at these that have little muscle, this happens quickly; at those who have enough flesh, this happens by jumping, and then returns by jumping.
Et par aventure avient a aucuns homes percussion ou casseure, et enfle li espaule d’un aposteme chaut, et cuide qu’elle est desaluee par ceu.	And by chance, some men suffer from impact or fracture, and the shoulder swells due to an abscess, and they believe that it is dislocated because of this.
Il covient donques que tu l’esprueves, tant que tu en soies certains; et adonques encomence la cure.	Therefore, you must test them until you are certain; then begin the treatment.
Et est conue li dislocations quant il est aval vers l’assele, et met difference entre l’espaule malade et la saine, et tu troveras entre lor diversiteit manifeste; et troveras au chief de l’espaule une fosse, et desoz l’assele au tochier le chief de l’espaule, ausi com se ce soit uns oes; et ne puet li malaides ramener sa main a son neis, ne movoir de nulz movemens; et ausi, s’elle est desaluee en haut, si n’est mie occultee, car tu le trueves manifestement au tochier; et ceste maniere de dislocation n’est mie fors a ramener, quant elle est novele, ou se li enfes est malaides.	And it is known how dislocations occur when they move towards the acromion, and one recognizes the difference between the diseased shoulder and the healthy one, you will find various clear distinctions between them; you will also find a depression at the head of the shoulder, from where to the base of the acromion as if it were an eye; the patient cannot bring their hand to their nose, nor can they move in any movements; similarly, if it is dislocated high up, it is not hidden either because you clearly find it at the base; and this way of dislocation does not allow bringing back when it's new, or when the child is sick.
Et li maniere est que li ministres lieve la main dou malaide en haut, puis met tes peuchas desoz l’assele, et lieve la jointure a force en haut au leu; et li ministres lieve la main, et l’estende en haut, pues le mette desoz; si venra hastanment.	And the method is that the minister lifts his hand from the malady at the top, then places his fingers on the shoulder blade, and raises the joint to its full extent at the top above him; and the minister lifts his hand and extends it up high, putting it under; if it comes quickly.
Et s’elle ne vient si com nos avons dit em mains jors aprés, si covient ke li malaides soit baigniez en aigue chaude; et li amenistre arosement mollifiant et assouajant, si com decoction de altee et de fenugrec et de mellilote en aigue, et soit amenistree; puis soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos, et mette on desoz l’assele un sto de lainne igal, ne trop mol ne trop dur, puis mette li mires son talon sus le sto, et lieve le chief de l’espaule vertuousement, et traie la main dou malaide; et uns autres ministres teigne lou chief dou malaide, si qu’il ne se mueve aval; celle espaule revient tout maintenant, et se tu vues si le ramoinne selonc ceste maniere: et est que tu faices estre present I home qui soit plus grans que li malaides; et soit drois devers lou costeit, et boute s’espaule desoz l’assele dou malaide, et lieve l’assele en haut, si que li malaides pende en l’ar; et uns autres ministres traie la main dou malaide aval devers lou ventre.	And if it does not come out as we have said after a few days, then the patient should be bathed in hot water. And apply soothing and restorative remedies to them; such as decoction of garlic, fenugreek and melilot in water, and they need to be applied; then dress the injured area with wool padding that is neither too soft nor too hard. Place a small cushion under their foot and place their heel on it, gently lift up the shoulder blade and pull the hand towards the patient; have another assistant press the top of the shoulder down firmly, so as not to let them move back. The shoulder now returns immediately in this manner: if you see that you have successfully reset it following this method: make sure there is someone bigger than the patient present at home during this process and position them straight towards the injured side, push the shoulder under the pillow of the patient, lift up the pillow and place their head upright so that the injured person hangs in the air. Have another assistant pull the hand away from the patient towards their stomach.
Et se li malaides est trop legiers, si pent avec lui aucune chose pesant, et li dislocation revient maintenant.	And if the patient is too weak, they cannot support anything heavy with him, and the dislocation returns immediately.
Et le ramoinne on ausi en autre maniere: et est c’on fiche I lonc tison en terre, dont li chiés soit ausi reons com I pistal, et ne soit ne trop gros ne trop graile; puis soit mis desoz lou malaide, mais k’il ait drapelz souef sus, et li malaides soit estans dou lonc dou fust; puis soit estendue sa main aval d’autre part forment, et li jointure revenra en son leu hastanment; et s’elle ne vuet revenir por toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si fai ceste cure: pren I tison de II bras de grant et IIII dois de large, qui ait le chief reont por mues entrer em parfont desoz l’assele, selonc ceste forme:	And resetting can also be done in other ways: and you stick the long coal into the ground, so that the shoulder is placed like a pistol, and it's neither too big nor too greasy; then place it under the patient, but with its head resting on something soft, and the shoulder remains at the same length of the fender; then extend your hand from below on the other side to form, and the joint will return to its place quickly; and if it doesn't return using all these things that we have said, you perform this treatment: take a stick of two arms wide and three inches thick, which has its head rounded so as to be able to enter through perfectly under the pit, according to this form:
puis lie sus le chief dou fust drapelz souez, que li fust ne blece lou malaide, puis le met desoz l’assele dou malaide; et estende som bras sus le fust dou lonc, et lie l’ajutoire sus le fust, et lou bras au chief de la main, puis met le bras sus .i. eschillon d’une eschiele dou large, et soit estendue li mains aval, et soit laissiez li cors pendans d’autre part: li jointure reva ens maintenant.	Then bind the head to the stick with a piece of cloth underneath, so that the stick does not bruise the patient's arm, then place the stick under the arm against the side; and extend your hand up along the stick from the elbow, and fix the shoulder on the stick, and the arm at the elbow joint, then place your arm on one of the stakes about the width of a thumb, and keep the other hand hanging down, leaving the body hanging from the opposite side: the joint will return to its place now.
Et quant elle est ens, en quel maniere que ce soit, si covient que tu mettes desoz l’assele une spere de laine igal, puis met l’emplaustre aparilliet de poudre dou molin, avec encens et aubun d’uef, sus toute l’espaule et entor, puis l’estrain desoz l’assele avenanment, et torne le liien sus l’emplaustre, et embraice la main a son col, et soit li mains demorans ensi. de la dislocation dou coute	From the dislocation of the shoulder joint
Saiches que li jointure dou coute est desaluee a poinnes, et a poinnes revient; et s’est desaluee de toutes pars, et meismement devant et derrier, et li dislocations n’est mie reponue, car on la voit bien et sent bien; et desalue selonc chescune figure. des dislocations de la hainche	On the dislocations of the hip

Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit; et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	And when the dislocation is in front, it should be extended immediately as far as possible, and according to what I said; and place the patient's pain on the wrong side, then press with the other hand, and extend down towards the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches; et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table; et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz; adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve; et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus; et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors; puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	And if the dislocation is at the back, it is not appropriate to extend the patient's head downwards or lift them from the ground. Instead, they should be in a position as though their hip was dislocated forwards, just like we said about lying on both hips; and they should lie on their stomach, with the band stretched out as we explained before, and apply pressure at the joint to the table; it will be correct when the patient extends their legs, and they are even; then adjust the knees, put in the plaster, tighten with one band, so that the hip does not move. And lie for three days or four, then reset them, and place the plaster again; and if you see that they are even, then tighten further like before, and let them rest for three more days; then reset them, and make them walk properly, until their limbs are comfortable.
de la dislocation dou genoil	Of the dislocation of the hip
Li genous est desaluez selonc .iij. manieres: c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier; et ne desalue point devant.	The hip joint can be dislocated in three ways: one might say inside and outside, and behind; and it does not dislocate forward.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez; et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez; puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment; et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement; et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie; et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	And the signs for this are that you instruct the patient to bend their leg at their knee. If they cannot bend it at their knee, then know they are dislocated; and the restoration of all is when you make the patient stand straight, stretch out their leg if they can, place your back against their buttocks, and set one foot on your feet; then grab their knee with your palms, draw it between your fingers, then bend both sides near the knee smoothly. And another attendant stretches their foot until the knees return to their place, and the signs are that they bend well their leg at their knee lightly; then apply plaster, and heat up the leg at the knee, and hold them together tightly for three or four days, then release them; do not move the patient to walk until the limbs are strengthened.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the limbs are not at all, administer strong extension, as we have said in the treatment of the hip, as long as it is sane.
de la dislocation dou talon	From the dislocation of the heel
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heels are sometimes partially dislocated and sometimes fully out, both inside and outside.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee: li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	And the signs are that the ankle is swollen and tries to move forward towards the part where it has been dislocated: the movement should be gentle, and one must gently extend it with their hands as soon as they sense it.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville; puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut; et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet; s’elle revient, c’est bien; se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient; et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide; puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet; puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent; puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	And when it is dislocated immediately, you must make the patient lie straight, and let them hold their leg up by supporting it from the ankle, above the ankle; then pull the foot towards your right hand, and then to your left twice. Then extend it upwards, and firmly push the foot up; do this two times, as we have said, while pushing and pulling on the foot. If it returns, that's good; if not, start over with the process, because it will return; and if it can't return like that, you must move the leg beneath their back to the ground, firmly place a stick between its thighs, and bind bandages around them so they don't hurt themselves; then shave the thigh of the injured leg, and have other helpers extend the foot towards their hands or knees, where they tie it near the neck of the foot; then evenly extend each helper's hand, and place the stick firmly between the thighs to keep the injured side when extending it; finally place mirrors equal to the dislocation at their hands, and have another helper shave the healthy leg below its knee, and the dislocation will return quickly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois; puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain; puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors; et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And when it is at the correct point, apply the plaster and bandage over it, keep it steady, tie the foot to the leg, watch that the ties near the ankle are not too tight; then leave it for two or three days. If they loosen with time, do so gradually. Then, release after the third day or fourth day, and allow the limb freedom for about four more days; if progress continues beyond this point, there is still a risk of re-dislocation.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when abscesses begin to drain, you should soothe them as we have said in other parts of the text, while they are still clean.
des dois	Of the cautery tool directed by fire, command the patient to let their hairs grow long and uniform; and if they start pricking at their base, keep the eyes steady so they don't move until they fully grow.
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the shoulders are dislocated, if they should be nicely extended for work, it is a simple task.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne; et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie; et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the dislocation is in no way at the back of the neck or at the feet, it is necessary that you have the patient sit on a flat surface like a table completely straight, and place your foot over what opens from these joints, then press with your foot until it heals; and when it is equal and doesn't open anymore, put under the sole of the foot a table for two shoulders, then hold steadily, and leave him for three days, then release him; and have him rest until he has recovered.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	regarding wounds and dislocations together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert: si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis; et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit; et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne; et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis; et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples; et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	When a wound occurs with dislocation and you wish to restore it, many times the patient dies: if you are not presumptuous in treatment, if you are not skilled in the art and have not used it for long periods, and if you are not pitiful and merciful but rather bold; then at first use things that soothe abscesses moderately, and leave the patient to God's mercy, if you do not see hope of healing; and when you see hope, immediately reset the limb in its place, as if the abscesses should burst and heal; and when the limb is in place, administer soothing remedies for abscesses, and treat the wound properly, with desiccated ointments; and if there's a break due to dislocation, and small bones are broken, bind them up, and do what we have told you about simple diseases; and refrain from entering into paths of fear according to what I said, for this befits you as per your Creator, and with the wisdom that arm you and your body.
Amen	Amen
